```
å±æ€§ï¼š
	method : æäº¤æ–¹å¼
	action : URL æäº¤ç›®çš„åœ°
	name   : è§„å®šè¡¨å•çš„åç§°
	target : è§„å®šåœ¨ä½•å¤„æ‰“å¼€ action URL
	enctypeï¼šç¼–ç æ–¹å¼
		application/x-www-form-urlencoded 	ï¼š HTMLé»˜è®¤æ–¹å¼

	é€šè¿‡ç‚¹å‡»submit æŒ‰é’®ï¼Œè§¦å‘è¡¨å•æäº¤æ“ä½œï¼Œä»è€Œä½¿é¡µé¢è·³è½¬åˆ°action URL æ‰€æŒ‡å‘çš„åœ°å€

	mySubmit(this) è¿”å›false åˆ™ä¸æäº¤è¡¨å•
```

```html

    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <title>è·å–formè¡¨å•çš„æ•°æ®</title>

  <div class="main">
      <form method="post" action="login.html" name="login" target="_blank" onsubmit="return mySubmit(this)">
          <label for="UserName"> ç”¨æˆ·å: </label>
          <input type="text" name="username" id="UserName" placeholder="è¯·è¾“å…¥ç”¨æˆ·å"><br>
          <label for="PassWord"> å¯† ç ï¼š </label>
          <input type="password" name="password" id="PassWord" placeholder="è¯·è¾“å…¥å¯†ç "><br>

      </form>
  </div>

<script>
      function mySubmit(form) {
        let formData = new FormData(form);
        let username = formData.get('username');
        let password = formData.get('password');
        console.log(username)
        console.log(password)
        console.log(document.querySelector("form").name);		// æ‰“å°è¡¨å•å
        return true ;  // å…è®¸è¡¨å•æäº¤
        return false ; // ä¸å…è®¸è¡¨å•æäº¤
      }
```

```html
    let formData = new FormData(form);
    console.log(formData.getAll("size"))
    return true ;
  }
</script>
</html>
```

# 02 CSS3

MDNç½‘å€ï¼šhttps://developer.mozilla.org/zh-CN/docs/Web/CSS/padding-inline-start

## CSS3åŸºç¡€

### èƒŒæ™¯çŸ¥è¯†

#### CSSå‘å±•å²

```
Cascading Style Sheet å±‚å æ ·å¼è¡¨

CSS 1.0 :
CSS 2.0	: DIV + CSS
CSS 2.1	: æµ®åŠ¨ã€å®šä½
```

\end{aligned}
$$

## CSS3é«˜çº§


##### è¿ç®—ç¬¦*2

##### 1 var

- [x] **[[Environment]] äº§ç”Ÿçš„æ¡ä»¶ï¼š**

```js

    let a = 0
    return function fin(){
        return ++a
    }

console.log(fa()) 		//2

```

**å‡½æ•°å®ä¾‹åˆ›å»ºå**ä¼šäº§ç”Ÿä¸€ä¸ªfa ï¼Œå®ƒçš„[[environment]]æŒ‡å‘finçš„è¯æ³•ä½œç”¨å¯¹è±¡ï¼Œè¯¥å¯¹è±¡å­˜åœ¨ä¸€ä¸ªå¤–éƒ¨è¯æ³•ç¯å¢ƒå¼•ç”¨æŒ‡å‘foutè¯æ³•ç¯å¢ƒå¯¹è±¡ï¼ŒåŒç†foutè¯æ³•ç¯å¢ƒå¯¹è±¡ä¸­å­˜åœ¨ä¸€ä¸ªå¤–éƒ¨è¯æ³•ç¯å¢ƒå¼•ç”¨æŒ‡å‘å…¨å±€è¯æ³•ç¯å¢ƒå¯¹è±¡ã€‚å¦‚ä¸‹å›¾

#### 7  **ç®­å¤´å‡½æ•°çš„this**

```
	ç®­å¤´å‡½æ•°çš„thisæŒ‡å‘å–å†³äºå¤–å±‚ä½œç”¨åŸŸä¸­çš„this
	å¤–å±‚ä½œç”¨åŸŸæˆ–å‡½æ•°çš„thisæŒ‡å‘è°ï¼Œç®­å¤´å‡½æ•°ä¸­çš„thisä¾¿æŒ‡å‘è°ã€‚
```

```js
        function Child() {
```

##### 3.4 resolve \ rejectå‡½æ•°å®ç°

```
ç»†èŠ‚1:  çŠ¶æ€åªèƒ½ä¿®æ”¹ä¸€æ¬¡ï¼Œæ•…éœ€è¦åšçŠ¶æ€åˆ¤æ–­ã€‚
```

```js
function resolve(data) {
    if (self.status !== PENDING) return 
    self.data = data
    self.status = RESOLVED
    if (self.callbacks.length > 0) {
        self.callbacks.forEach(item => {
            item.onResolved()
        })
    }
}
```

```js
function handler_async(callback) {
    try {
        let res = callback(self.info);
        if (res instanceof Mypromise) {
            res.then(
                (data) => {
                    r(data);
                },
                (err) => {
                    j(err);
                }
            );
        } else {
            r(res); 
        }
    } catch (e) {
        j(e);  //ä¸­æ–­
        if(e instanceof Error)throw Error(e);   
    }
}
```

##### 2.7 then /catchçš„å®ç°

```
1. then è¿”å›çš„æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªpromise
2. å½“å‰thenè¿”å›çš„promiseä¸æŒ‡å®šå›è°ƒå‡½æ•°è¿”å›çš„Promiseä¹‹é—´çš„é—®é¢˜å¤„ç†
3. undefinedä½œä¸ºå‚æ•°è¿›è¡Œä¼ é€’æ—¶ï¼Œä¸ä¼šæ”¹å˜é»˜è®¤å‚æ•°å€¼
```

#### 3 Promiseå¤ç°

##### 3.1 æ ¸å¿ƒå®ç°

```js
(function (window) {
  const A = "A1";
  const B = "B1";
  const C = "C1";
  function Mypromise(exec) {
    let self = this;
    self.info = undefined;
    self.status = A;
    self.callbacks = [];
    function handler(info, status, callback) {
      if (self.status != A) return;
      self.info = info;
      self.status = status;
      if (self.callbacks.length > 0) {
        self.callbacks.forEach((item) => {
          setTimeout(() => {
            item[callback]();
          });
        });
      }
    }
    function resolve(data) {
      handler(data, B, "OnResolved");
    }
    function reject(err) {
      handler(err, C, "OnRejected");
    }
    try {
      exec(resolve, reject);
    } catch (e) {
      reject(e);
    }
  }
  window.Mypromise = Mypromise;
  Mypromise.prototype.then = function (OnResolve=(data)=>{return data}, OnReject=(err)=>{throw err}) {
    let self = this;
    return new Mypromise((r, j) => {
      function handler_async(callback) {
        try {
          let res = callback(self.info);
          if (res instanceof Mypromise) {
            res.then(
              (data) => {
                r(data);
              },
              (err) => {
                j(err);
              }
            );
          } else {
            r(res); // è¿”å›ç»“æœä¸ä¸ºPromiseï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆå°±å¯¹å…¶è¿”å›å€¼è¿›è¡Œå¤„ç†
          }
        } catch (e) {
          j(e);
          if(e instanceof Error)throw Error(e);  
        }
      }
      if (self.status == B) {
        setTimeout(() => {
          handler_async(OnResolve);
        });
      } else if (self.status == C) {
        setTimeout(() => {
          handler_async(OnReject);
        });
      } else {
        self.callbacks.push({
          OnResolved: () => {
            handler_async(OnResolve);
          },
          OnRejected: () => {
            handler_async(OnReject);
          },
        });
      }
    });
  };
  Mypromise.prototype.catch = function (OnReject){
     this.then(undefined,OnReject)
  }
})(window);
```

##### 2.resolve/rejectç±»æ–¹æ³•

```js
  MyPromise.resolve = function (value){
    return new MyPromise((r,j)=>{
        if(value instanceof MyPromise){
            value.then(r,j) ;
        }else{
            r(value) ;
        }
    })
  }

  MyPromise.reject = function(reason){
    return new MyPromise((r,j)=>{
        j(reason) ;
        if(reason instanceof MyPromise){
          reason.catch((err)=>{
            setTimeout(()=>{throw Error(err) ;})
          })
        }
    })
  }
```

è¿™ä¹ˆå†™çš„åŸå› æ˜¯æ–‡æ¡£çš„è¦æ±‚

```js
// const p = MyPromise.resolve("data")
// const p1 = MyPromise.resolve(MyPromise.resolve("r - r"))
// const p2 = MyPromise.resolve(MyPromise.reject("r - j"))
// let pp =  p.then((data)=>{console.log("p data",data)},(err)=>{console.log("p err",err)})
```

##### 3.all/raceç±»æ–¹æ³•

```js
Promise.all = function (promisesList) { 
    let lists = new Array(promisesList.length)
    let counterflag = promisesList.length
    return new Promise((resolve,reject)=>{
        promisesList.forEach((item,index)=>{
            Promise.resolve(item).then(   // æ‹…å¿ƒpromisListä¸æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªPromisedå¯¹è±¡
                value =>{
                    lists[index] = value
                    counterflag -=1

                    //å¦‚æœå…¨éƒ¨æˆåŠŸè°ƒç”¨resolveã€‚
                    if(!counterflag){
                        resolve(lists)
                    }
                },
                err =>{
                    reject(err)
                }
            )
        })
    })
}

Promise.race = function (promisesList) { 
    let successflag = false
    return new Promise((resolve,reject)=>{
        promisesList.forEach((item,index)=>{
            Promise.resolve(item).then(   // æ‹…å¿ƒpromisListä¸æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªPromisedå¯¹è±¡
                (data)=>{
                    if(!successflag){
                        resolve(data)
                        successflag = true
                    }
                },err=>{
                    reject(err)
                })
        })
    })
}
```



##### 4.è‡ªå®šä¹‰æ–¹æ³•

```js
Promise.resolveDelay = function (value,timeout=0){
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        if (value instanceof Promise) {
            setTimeout(()=>{
                value.then(resolve, reject)
            },timeout)
        } else {
            setTimeout(()=>{
                resolve(value)
            },timeout) 
        }
    }) 
}
Promise.rejectDealy= function (reason,timeout=0){
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        setTimeout(()=>{
            reject(reason)
        },timeout)
    })
}
```



#### 4 ES6Class

```js
(function (window) {
    const PENDING = 'pending'
    const RESOLVED = 'fulfilled'
    const REJECTED = 'failure'
    class Promise {
        constructor(executor) {
            let self = this   //å­˜å‚¨å½“å‰Promiseå¯¹è±¡ï¼Œä¾›é—­åŒ…ä½¿ç”¨
            self.status = PENDING
            self.data = undefined
            self.callbacks = [] // æ¯ä¸ªåŸç”Ÿçš„ç»“æ„ä¸ºï¼š{onResolved(){},onRejected(){}}
            function resolve(data) {}
            function reject(err) {}
            //æ‰§è¡Œå™¨å¼‚å¸¸å¤„ç†
            try {
                executor(resolve, reject)
            } catch (e) {
                reject(e)
            }
        }
        //promise åŸå‹å¯¹è±¡ä¸Šçš„æ–¹æ³•
        then = function (onResolved = (data) => { return data }, onRejected = (err) => { throw err }) {}
        catch = function (onRejected) {}
        // Promiseå‡½æ•°å¯¹è±¡çš„æ–¹æ³•
        static resolve = function (value) {}
        static reject = function (reason) { }
        static race = function (promisesList) {}
        static all = function (promisesList) {}
        static resolveDelay = function (value, timeout = 0) {}
        static rejectDealy = function (reason, timeout = 0) {}
    }
    window.Promise = Promise
}(window))
```



#### 5 asyncå’Œawait

- async ç”¨æ¥å®šä¹‰ä¸€ä¸ªå¼‚æ­¥å‡½æ•°

  è¯­æ³•ï¼š

  â€‹	async function funName(params){ ..... }

  â€‹	async å‡½æ•°è¿”å›promiseå¯¹è±¡,å› ä¸ºreturn çš„ç»“æœä¼šè¢«é»˜è®¤åŒ…è£…æˆPromise



- await ç”¨æ¥ç­‰å¾…ä¸€ä¸ªæˆåŠŸçš„Promiseå¯¹è±¡ï¼Œ

  è¯­æ³•ï¼š

  â€‹	[return_value] = await expression

  â€‹	**è¡¨è¾¾å¼** expression æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªPromise æˆ–ä»»ä½•è¦ç­‰å¾…çš„å€¼

  â€‹	**è¿”å›å€¼** è¿”å›Promiseå¯¹è±¡çš„å¤„ç†ç»“æœï¼Œè‹¥ç­‰å¾…çš„ä¸æ˜¯Promiseå¯¹è±¡ï¼Œåˆ™è¿”å›è¯¥å€¼æœ¬èº«ã€‚

â€‹	ç¬¬ä¸€è¦ä¹‰ï¼šç­‰å¾…ä»£ç æ‰§è¡Œå®Œæ¯•

â€‹	ç¬¬äºŒè¦ä¹‰ï¼šä»£ç æ‰§è¡Œçš„**æˆåŠŸçš„ç»“æœ**è¿›è¡Œæ¥æ”¶ï¼Œå€˜è‹¥å¤±è´¥ï¼Œåˆ™éœ€è¦ä½¿ç”¨try-catch



```js
function fn(){
    return new Promise((resolve,reject)=>{
        setTimeout(()=>{
            resolve("OK statue")
            reject("No More")
        },1000)
    })
}

async function Use(){
    try{
        const result = await fn()
        console.log("Promiseå¯¹è±¡æˆåŠŸ----- ",result)
        return result
    }catch(err){
        console.log("Promiseå¯¹è±¡å¤±è´¥----- ",err)
    }
}

let ok = Use()
```



#### 6  JS å¼‚æ­¥ä¹‹å®é˜Ÿåˆ—å’Œå¾®é˜Ÿåˆ—

JS ä¸­ç”¨æ¥**å­˜å‚¨å¾…æ‰§è¡Œå›è°ƒå‡½æ•°**çš„é˜Ÿåˆ—åŒ…å«2 ä¸ªä¸åŒç‰¹å®šçš„åˆ—é˜Ÿ

1ã€å®åˆ—é˜Ÿ: ç”¨æ¥ä¿å­˜å¾…æ‰§è¡Œçš„å®ä»»åŠ¡(å›è°ƒ), æ¯”å¦‚: å®šæ—¶å™¨å›è°ƒ/DOM äº‹ä»¶å›è°ƒ/ajax å›è°ƒ

*2ã€*å¾®åˆ—é˜Ÿ: ç”¨æ¥ä¿å­˜å¾…æ‰§è¡Œçš„å¾®ä»»åŠ¡( å›è°ƒ), æ¯”å¦‚: promise çš„å›è°ƒ/MutationObserver çš„å›è°ƒ

3ã€JS æ‰§è¡Œæ—¶ä¼šåŒºåˆ«è¿™2 ä¸ªé˜Ÿåˆ—

ã€€ã€€3.1ã€€JS å¼•æ“é¦–å…ˆå¿…é¡»å…ˆæ‰§è¡Œæ‰€æœ‰çš„åˆå§‹åŒ–åŒæ­¥ä»»åŠ¡ä»£ç 

ã€€ã€€3.2ã€€æ¯æ¬¡å‡†å¤‡å–å‡ºç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå®ä»»åŠ¡æ‰§è¡Œå‰, éƒ½è¦å°†æ‰€æœ‰çš„å¾®ä»»åŠ¡ä¸€ä¸ªä¸€ä¸ªå–å‡º**æ¥æ‰§è¡Œ**



```js
setTimeout(()=>{
    console.log("timeout callback1")
    Promise.resolve(3).then(value=>{
        console.log("Promise OnResolved ",value)
    })
},0)
Promise.resolve("1").then((data)=>{console.log("Promise OnResolved ",data)})
setTimeout(()=>{
    console.log("timeout callback2")
},0)

Promise.resolve("2").then((data)=>{console.log("Promise OnResolved ",data)})
```

```js
ä¿®æ”¹box çš„classå±æ€§
.b2{
	border:;
}
let box = document.querySelector(".box") ;
let btn = document.querySelector("input") ;
btn.addEventListener('click',function () {
    toggleClass(box,"b2")
}) ;

function toggleClass(elem,classAttr) {
    hasClass(elem,classAttr)?removeClass(elem,classAttr):addClass(elem,classAttr) ;
}
function addClass(elem,classAttr) {
    !hasClass(elem,classAttr)? elem.className +=" "+classAttr : null;
}
function removeClass(elem,classAttr) {
    hasClass(elem,classAttr)? elem.className = elem.className.replace(classAttr,"").trim(): null ;
}
function hasClass(elem,classAttr) {
    return  new RegExp(`\\b${classAttr}\\b`).test(elem.className) ;
}
```

```js
/*
       * é—®é¢˜ä¸€ï¼š
       *    äº‹ä»¶æ·»åŠ callbackå‡½æ•°çš„å…¼å®¹æ€§
       * é—®é¢˜äºŒï¼š
       *    äº‹ä»¶æ·»åŠ callbackå‡½æ•°çš„this æŒ‡å‘
       * é—®é¢˜ä¸‰ï¼š
       *    callbackå‡½æ•°å¾—event å‚æ•°å…¼å®¹æ€§
* */
function bind(elem,eventName,callback) {
    if(elem.addEventListener){
        elem.addEventListener(eventName,callback,false)
    }else{
        // IE8ä¹‹ä¸‹å…¼å®¹æ–¹å¼
        elem.attachEvent("on"+eventName,function () {
            // åœ¨åŒ¿åå‡½æ•°ä¸­è°ƒç”¨callback
            callback.call(elem)  //æ˜¾ç¤ºç»‘å®š
        })
    }
}

bind(document.getElementsByTagName("div")[0],"click",function (event) {
    if(!event){
        event = window.event ;
    }
    event = event||window.event
    alert(this)
})
```

```js
  function whell(event) {
     // IE8- å…¼å®¹è®¾ç½®
     event = event || window.event ;
     // ç«ç‹ä¸æ”¯æŒçš„å±æ€§wheelDeltaï¼Œç«ç‹æ‰“å°undefined
     // ç«ç‹æ”¯æŒçš„å±æ€§detail , å…¶ä»–æµè§ˆå™¨æ‰“å° 0
     var flag = whell_direct(event.wheelDelta)||whell_direct(-(event.detail)) ;
     handler(flag)

     // å–æ¶ˆäº‹ä»¶é»˜è®¤è¡Œä¸º
     event.preventDefault||event.preventDefault() //
     return false
  }

  // å…¼å®¹ç«ç‹æ»šåŠ¨ç»‘å®šäº‹ä»¶
  function EventBind_mouseWheel(elem,func){
    // fireFox æ»šè½®ç»‘å®š
    elem.addEventListener && elem.addEventListener("DOMMouseScroll",func,false) ;
    // Chrom   æ»šè½®ç»‘å®š
    elem.onmousewheel = func ;
  }

  EventBind_mouseWheel(g,whell) ;
</script>
</html>
```

###### é”®ç›˜äº‹ä»¶

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <title>é”®ç›˜äº‹ä»¶</title>
    <style>
        *{margin:0px;padding: 0px}
        .box{
            width: 100px;
            height: 100px;
            background-color: #a18cd1;
            position: absolute;
        }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="box"></div>
</body>

<script defer>

    var box = document.querySelector(".box") ;
    function handler(code){
        switch (code) {
          case 37 :
             box.style.left = (isNaN(parseInt(box.style.left))?0:parseInt(box.style.left)) - 10 + "px" ;
             break;
          case 38 :
            box.style.top = (isNaN(parseInt(box.style.top))?0:parseInt(box.style.top)) - 10 + "px" ;
            break;
          case 39 :
            box.style.left = (isNaN(parseInt(box.style.left))?0:parseInt(box.style.left)) + 10 +"px" ;
            break;
          case 40 :
            box.style.top = (isNaN(parseInt(box.style.top))?0:parseInt(box.style.top)) + 10 +"px" ;
            break;
        }
    }

    document.addEventListener("keydown",function (event) {
      event = event||window.event ;
      if(event.keyCode>=37 && event.keyCode<=40){
         
        handler(event.keyCode)
      }else{
        return false ;
      }
    })
</script>
</html>
```

#### é˜²æŠ–èŠ‚æµ

```js
é˜²æŠ–ï¼š
	åœ¨å‰ç«¯æœ‰ä¸€äº›äº‹ä»¶ï¼Œä¸€æ—¦è¢«ä¿ƒå‘ï¼Œå°±æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªçŸ­æ—¶é«˜é¢‘ç‡è§¦å‘çš„ç‰¹æ€§ã€‚
    æ­¤æ—¶æˆ‘ä»¬åˆæœ‰ç›‘è§†è¯¥ç±»äº‹ä»¶çš„éœ€æ±‚ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯æˆ‘åªæ˜¯å¸Œæœ›ç›‘è§†å®ƒæœ€åä¸€æ¬¡çš„äº‹ä»¶ã€‚è¿™æ—¶å€™å°±å¯ä»¥ç”¨é˜²æŠ–
    é˜²æŠ–æŒ‡çš„æ˜¯å½“äº‹ä»¶åœæ­¢è§¦å‘ä¸€æ®µæ—¶é—´åï¼Œå¦‚æœæ²¡æœ‰åœ¨è¢«è§¦å‘æ‰ä¼šæœ€ç»ˆæ‰§è¡Œå¯¹è¯¥äº‹ä»¶çš„å¤„ç†å‡½æ•°ã€‚
èŠ‚æµï¼š
	å½“æŸä¸ªæ“ä½œæ˜¯è¿ç»­æ€§æ‰§è¡Œçš„æ—¶å€™ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬é€šè¿‡æŸç§æ–¹å¼ï¼Œé™ä½è¯¥æ“ä½œçš„æ‰§è¡Œé¢‘ç‡ï¼Œè¿™å°±æ˜¯èŠ‚æµã€‚
	
function debounce(handler, delayTime) {
    let timer = null;
    return (...args) => {
        if (timer) {
            //å¦‚æœtimeræœ‰å€¼
            clearTimeout(timer); //å¯¹å…¶è¿›è¡Œæ¸…é™¤
            timer = setTimeout(() => {
                handler(...args);
            }, delayTime);
        } else {
            timer = setTimeout(() => {
                handler(...args);
            }, delayTime);
        }
    };
}

let freash = debounce(function(){console.log("hello");},200)
freash()
freash()
function throttle(handler,dalaytime) {
    let timer = null;
    return (...args)=>{
        if (timer) {
            return;
        }
        timer = setTimeout(() => {
            //æ‰§è¡Œæ“ä½œ(ä½¿ç”¨applyé‡æ–°ç»‘å®šthisçš„æŒ‡å‘)
            handler(...args)
            timer = null;
        },dalaytime)
    }
}

let thort = throttle(function(){log("hellow")},2000)
```

```html
                <a href="javascript:;">å›¾åƒä¼˜åŒ–</a>
                <a href="javascript:;">æ”¶è—å¤¹</a>
                <a href="javascript:;">é‚®ä»¶</a>
                <a href="javascript:;">htaccesså¯†ç </a>
                <a href="javascript:;">æ¢¯åº¦å›¾åƒ</a>
                <a href="javascript:;">æŒ‰é’®ç”Ÿæˆå™¨</a>
            </div>
            <div class="collapsed">
                <span class="menuspan">æ”¯æŒæˆ‘ä»¬</span>
                <a href="javascript:;">æ¨èæˆ‘ä»¬</a>
                <a href="javascript:;">è¿æ¥æˆ‘ä»¬</a>
                <a href="javascript:;">ç½‘ç»œèµ„æº</a>
            </div>
            <div class="collapsed">
                <span class="menuspan">åˆä½œä¼™ä¼´</span>
                <a href="javascript:;">jså·¥å…·åŒ…</a>
                <a href="javascript:;">CSSé©±åŠ¨</a>
                <a href="javascript:;">CodingForums</a>
            </div>

    </div>

<script defer>
   let menuspan = document.querySelectorAll(".menuspan") ;
   var currOpen = document.querySelectorAll(".menuspan")[0].parentNode ;
   menuspan.forEach((item)=>{
     item.addEventListener("click",function (event) {
        if(this.parentNode == currOpen){  // å…³é—­çš„æ˜¯å½“å‰æ´»åŠ¨çš„çª—å£
          toggleClass(this.parentNode,"collapsed",10) ;
          currOpen = null ;
        }else{
          if(currOpen!=null){
            toggleClass(currOpen,"collapsed",10)
          }
            currOpen = this.parentNode ;
            toggleClass(this.parentNode,"collapsed",20)
        }
     })
   }) ;

    function toggleClass(elem,classAttr,speed) {
      let begin = elem.offsetHeight ;
      //ä¼¸ç¼©æ ¸å¿ƒ
      hasClass(elem,classAttr)?removeClass(elem,classAttr):addClass(elem,classAttr) ;
      let end = elem.offsetHeight ;
      elem.style.height = begin+ "px"
      move(elem,"height",end,speed,()=> {elem.style.height = ""}) ;
    }
    // å»¶æ—¶åŠ¨ç”»
   function move(elem,attr,target,speed,callback) {
     let src = parseInt(elem.style[attr]) ;
     let add1 = parseInt( (target - src)/speed ) ;
     let add2 = (target -src)%speed ;

     for (let i = 0 ;i<speed;i++){
       setTimeout(()=>{
         elem.style[attr] = parseInt(elem.style[attr]) + add1 + "px" ;
       },i*30)
     }
     setTimeout(()=>{
       elem.style[attr] = parseInt(elem.style[attr]) + add2 + "px" ;
       callback()
     },speed*30)
   }
    function addClass(elem,classAttr) {
       !hasClass(elem,classAttr)? elem.className +=" "+classAttr : null;
    }
    function removeClass(elem,classAttr) {
        hasClass(elem,classAttr)? elem.className = elem.className.replace(classAttr,"").trim(): null ;
    }
    function hasClass(elem,classAttr) {
      return  new RegExp(`\\b${classAttr}\\b`).test(elem.className) ;
    }

</script>
</html>
```

#### åŒå‘ç»‘å®šåŸç†

```html
<div id="app">

<script>
     window.data = {}
     var Oin = document.querySelector("#password");
     var Oout = document.querySelector("#showData")
     // Page æ•°æ®è¾“å…¥ç»‘å®š
     Oin.addEventListener("input",function(e){
```

#### åˆ—è¡¨è¿‡æ»¤

```html
<div id="app">
    <input type="text" v-model="keyword" @keyup.enter="ufilter" placeholder="å…³é”®è¯æŸ¥è¯¢">  
    <ul v-for="item in list" :key="item">
        <li>{{ item }}</li>
    </ul>
</div>
<script>
	var vm = new Vue({
		data: {
			keyword:"",
            persons:["é©¬å†¬æ¢…","æ¢…é•¿è‹","è‹é—¨è¾¾æ‹‰","æ‹‰ä¸æ‹‰å¤š"],
            lists:[]
		},
        computed:{
            list:{
                get(){
                    if(this.lists.length==0){
                        return this.persons
                    }
                    return this.lists
                },
                set(value){
                    this.lists = value   
                }
            }
        },
        methods: {
            ufilter(){
                this.list = this.persons.filter((item)=>{
                    if(item.includes(this.keyword)){
                        return true
                    }
                })
            },
        },  
	})
    vm.$mount("#app")
</script>
```

#### åˆ—è¡¨æ’åº

```html
<div id="app">
    <input type="text" v-model="keyword" @keyup.enter="ufilter" placeholder="å…³é”®è¯æŸ¥è¯¢"> 
    <button @click="ascending"> å‡åº</button>
    <button @click="decending"> é™åº</button>
    <ul v-for="item in list" :key="item">
        <li>{{ item }}</li>
    </ul>
</div>
<script>
	var vm = new Vue({
		data: {
			keyword:"",
            persons:[["é©¬å†¬æ¢…","18"],["æ¢…é•¿è‹","34"],["è‹é—¨è¾¾æ‹‰","16"],["æ‹‰ä¸æ‹‰å¤š","32"]],
            lists:[]
		},
        computed:{
            list:{
                get(){
                    if(this.lists.length==0){
                        return this.persons
                    }
                    return this.lists
                },
                set(value){
                    this.lists = value   
                }
            }
        },
        methods: {
            ufilter(){
                this.list = this.persons.filter((item)=>{ return item[0].includes(this.keyword)}) // æ•°ç»„å“åº”å¼
            },
            decending(){
                this.list = this.list.sort((a,b)=>{return b[1]-a[1]})    
            },
            ascending(){
                this.list = this.list.sort((a,b)=>{ return a[1]-b[1]}) 	
            } 
        },  
	})
    vm.$mount("#app")
</script>
```

#### æ—¶é—´è¿‡æ»¤å™¨æ¨¡å—å°è£…

```js
export function formatDate(date, fmt) {
  if (/(y+)/.test(fmt)) {
    fmt = fmt.replace(RegExp.$1, (date.getFullYear() + '').substr(4 - RegExp.$1.length));
  }
  let o = {
    'M+': date.getMonth() + 1,
    'd+': date.getDate(),
    'h+': date.getHours(),
    'm+': date.getMinutes(),
    's+': date.getSeconds()
  };
  for (let k in o) {
    if (new RegExp(`(${k})`).test(fmt)) {
      let str = o[k] + '';
      fmt = fmt.replace(R egExp.$1, (RegExp.$1.length === 1) ? str : padLeftZero(str));
    }
  }
  return fmt;
};
function padLeftZero (str) {
  return ('00' + str).substr(str.length);
};
```

```js

æˆ‘ä»¬æœ‰å¤§é‡çš„ç¬¬ä¸‰æ–¹åº“æ–‡ä»¶æ²¡æœ‰å¿…è¦è‡ªå·±è¿›è¡Œä¹¦å†™
æ¯”å¦‚moment.js
```

#### æŒ‡ä»¤åè§„åˆ™

- [x] $on

```html
// App.vue

    <div id="app" class="athere">
       <School ref="Sc01"/>
    </div>
</template>
<script>

    name: "App",
    methods:{
        getSchhoName(msg){
            console.log("APP");
            console.log(msg);
        }
    },mounted(){
        this.$refs.Sc01.$on("getSchhoName",this.getSchhoName)      			// Schoolç»„ä»¶äº‹ä»¶ç›‘å¬
    },
    components: {
       Student
    }
};
```

```html
         return { schoolName: "æµ™å·¥å¤§"} 
    },

        send(){
            this.$emit("getSchhoName",this.schoolName)			/// Schoolç»„ä»¶å‘å‡ºä¸€ä¸ªäº‹ä»¶
```

mixin.js

```js
const mixin = {
    data() {
         return { schoolName: "æµ™å·¥å¤§minin", address: "å±å³°minxin" } 
    },
    methods: {
        show(){
            console.log("mixin_show")
        }
    },mounted(){
        console.log("mixin_mounted")
        this.show()
    }
}
export default mixin;
```

school.vue

```html
<script>
import mixin from "./minxin.js"							// å¯¼å…¥
export default {
    name :"School",
    mixins:[mixin],										// æ··å…¥
    methods:{
        show(){											
            console.log("school_show")
        }
    },mounted(){										// éªŒè¯ 2
        console.log("school_mounted")					// éªŒè¯ 3
        this.show()
    }
}
</script>
```

```js
    routes:[
        {
            path:"/home",	  // åˆ‡æ¢è·¯ç”±çš„ç›®æ ‡
            component:Home,	  // å¯¹åº”ç›®æ ‡çš„å±•ç¤ºç»„ä»¶
```

### å†å²è®°å½•æ¨¡å¼

#### history æ¨¡å¼


```js
// å¾®å‹æœåŠ¡å™¨

const history = require('connect-history-api-fallback');

const app = express()
app.use(history())
app.use(express.static(__dirname+'/static'))

app.listen(5005,(err)=>{
	if(!err) console.log('æœåŠ¡å™¨å¯åŠ¨æˆåŠŸäº†ï¼')
```

### GET ä¼ å‚

## æ–‡ä»¶ä¸Šä¼ 

### File å¯¹è±¡ç›´æ¥ä¸Šä¼ 

```
æ–‡ä»¶æ¥æºï¼š
	input[type=file]
	
åŸç†:
	1. è·å–inputçš„files
	2. å°†filesåˆ†åˆ«æ”¾å…¥formData
	3. ä½¿ç”¨xhrè¿›è¡Œå‘é€å³å¯
```

```js
å‰ç«¯ä»£ç ï¼š
	// å®šä½inputæ ‡ç­¾
    let input = document.querySelector("#file");
    //  è·å¾—ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªæ–‡ä»¶
	let file = input.files[0];
	//  åˆ›å»ºxhrå®ä¾‹å¯¹è±¡
    this.xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
    this.xhr.open("POST", "http://localhost:8080/cros/students");
	// åˆ›å»ºformDataå®ä¾‹å¯¹è±¡
    let fm = new FormData()
    // åˆ†è¯æ”¾å…¥ä¸¤ä¸ªæ–‡ä»¶
    fm.append("file", file);
    fm.append("file2", file);
	// è¿›è¡Œå‘é€

    this.xhr.onreadystatechange = this.xhrstatechange;

```

```js
åç«¯ä»£ç :
    const express = require('express')
    const fs = require('fs')
    const multiparty = require('multiparty')
    const app = express()
    
    app.post('/students', (req, res) => {
        // æ ¸å¿ƒä»£ç 
        // åˆ›å»ºformå¯¹è±¡
        let form = new multiparty.Form();
        // formè§£æ
        form.parse(req, function (err, fields, files) {
            try {
                console.log(files);
                let inputFile = files.file[0];
                let newPath = "C:/Users/DingZhiQiang/Desktop" + "/" + inputFile.originalFilename;
                // ä¿å­˜æ–‡ä»¶åˆ°æœåŠ¡å™¨æŒ‡å®šä½ç½®
                fs.renameSync(inputFile.path, newPath);
                res.send({ data: "ä¸Šä¼ æˆåŠŸï¼" });
            } catch (err) {
                console.log(err);
                res.send({ err: "ä¸Šä¼ å¤±è´¥ï¼" });
            };
        })
    })
    app.listen(5000, (err) => {
        if (!err) console.log('æœåŠ¡å™¨1å¯åŠ¨æˆåŠŸäº†,è¯·æ±‚å­¦ç”Ÿä¿¡æ¯åœ°å€ä¸ºï¼šhttp://localhost:5000/students');
    })
```

```js
     // base64 è§£ç 
     let byteString = window.atob(dataURI.split(",")[1]);
 	 // åˆ›å»ºç©ºé—´
     let ab = new ArrayBuffer(byteString.length);
	 // MIMEç±»å‹
     let mimeString = dataURI.split(",")[0].split(":")[1].split(";")[0];
     let ia = new Uint8Array(ab);
     for (let i = 0; i < byteString.length; i++) {
         ia[i] = byteString.charCodeAt(i); //æŒ‡å®šä½ç½®çš„Unicodeå­—ç¬¦ç¼–ç 
     }
     // è¿”å›Blobå®ä¾‹
```
